"Assobot Goku" first appeared in Weekly Shounen Magazine in issue 4/5 2002, and has since then been made into an animated series called "Assobot Senki Goku" (The Assobot Fighting Chronicles, Goku).

[25/9/2025, 7:28:31 p.Â m.] +54 9 11 3151-8889 ~Downtex > import { getContentType, downloadContentFromMessage } from '@adiwajshing/baileys'

const handler = async (sock, m, args, groupMetadata) => {
  if (!m.isGroup) return m.reply('Este comando solo funciona en grupos.')

  const participants = groupMetadata.participants.map(p => p.id)
  const mentionJid = participants.filter(p => p !== sock.user.id)

  // Si el mensaje es una respuesta a un medio (sticker, imagen, video, etc)
  if (m.quoted) {
    const count = parseInt(args[0])
    if (isNaN(count) || count > 30) return m.reply('Especifica cuÃ¡ntas veces (mÃ¡x 30)')

    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      await sock.sendMessage(m.chat, {
        forward: m.quoted.fakeObj,
        mentions: mentionJid
      }, { quoted: m })
    }
    return
  }

  // Si es texto plano: #spamtag mensaje 5
  const [_, ...rest] = args
  const text = rest.slice(0, -1).join(' ')
  const count = parseInt(rest.slice(-1)[0])

  if (!text || isNaN(count)) return m.reply('Uso: #spamtag mensaje 5')
  if (count > 30) return m.reply('MÃ¡ximo 30 repeticiones.')

  const finalText = (text + '\n').repeat(count)

  await sock.sendMessage(m.chat, {
    text: finalText.trim(),
    mentions: mentionJid
  }, { quoted: m })
}

export default {
  command: /^#?spamtag$/i,
  tags: ['grupos'],
  admin: true,
  group: true,
  handler
}
